<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вязать.html>вяза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навязать.html>навяза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navjazátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вязать.html>вяза́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навязывать.html>навя́зывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tie <i>(on)</i>, to fasten <i> (to)</i></li>
<li>to make <i>(a number of)</i>, to knit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навязать.html>навяза́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:узел.html>узло́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navjazátʹ</b> uzlóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a lot of knots</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навязать.html>навяза́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:носок.html>носко́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navjazátʹ</b> noskóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to knit a lot of socks</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to impose <i>(on)</i>, to thrust <i>(on)</i>, to foist <i>(off)</i> <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навязать.html>навяза́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воля.html>во́лю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navjazátʹ</b> svojú vólju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to impose/dictate one's will <i>(on)</i></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продавец.html>продаве́ц</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:навязать.html>навяза́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неисправный.html>неиспра́вный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:агрегат.html>агрега́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prodavéc <b>navjazál</b> jej neisprávnyj agregát</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the salesman foisted (off) the faulty machine on her</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вя<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>за́ть</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навязывать.html>навя́зывать</a> (11101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навязать.html>навяза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навязывать.html>навя́зывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navjázyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навязать.html>навяза́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tie <i>(on)</i>, to fasten <i> (to)</i></li>
<li>to make <i>(a number of)</i>, to knit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навязывать.html>навя́зывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:узел.html>узло́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navjázyvatʹ</b> uzlóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a lot of knots</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навязывать.html>навя́зывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:носок.html>носко́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navjázyvatʹ</b> noskóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to knit a lot of socks</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to impose <i>(on)</i>, to thrust <i>(on)</i>, to foist <i>(off)</i> <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навязывать.html>навя́зывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воля.html>во́лю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navjázyvatʹ</b> svojú vólju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to impose/dictate one's will <i>(on)</i></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продавец.html>продаве́ц</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:навязывать.html>навя́зывает</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неисправный.html>неиспра́вный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:агрегат.html>агрега́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prodavéc <b>navjázyvajet</b> jej neisprávnyj agregát</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the salesman is foisting (off) the faulty machine on her</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нагайка.html>нага́йка</a> (30989)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">нога́йский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nogájskij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Nogai</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагайка.html>нага́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagájka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагайка.html>нага́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагайка.html>нага́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагайка.html>нага́ек</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наган.html>нага́н</a> (10953)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Named after the original Belgian designers Léon and Émile <b>Nagant</b> (<span class="IPA">/naˈɡɑ̃/</span>). Officially was called <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:револьвер.html>револьве́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:система.html>систе́мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наган.html>нага́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">revolʹvér sistémy Nagána</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<ol><li>a Nagant M1895 revolver <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a seven-shot, gas-seal revolver designed and produced by Belgian industrialist Léon Nagant for the Russian Empire.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***наглец.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наглец.html>нагле́ц</a> (17670)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наглый.html>на́глый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">náglyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ец</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наглец.html>нагле́ц</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagléc</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наглец.html>наглеца́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наглец.html>наглецы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наглец.html>наглецо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> impudent / insolent fellow</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нагой.html>наг</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ле́ц</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 5b  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-нагл-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ец</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***нагло.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наглый.html>на́гло</a> (8767)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">наглъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naglŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*naglъ</i>. Per Vasmer, cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">अञ्जसा</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">añjasā</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soon, suddenly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">अञ्जस्</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">añjas</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">instantly, quickly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌰𐌽𐌰𐌺𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">anaks</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">suddenly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наглый.html>на́гло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">náglo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>impertinently, impudently
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:однажды.html>одна́жды</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:недолго.html>недо́лго</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мая</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наглый.html>на́гло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:напроситься.html>напроси́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:провожать.html>провожа́ть</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">i vot odnáždy ja, nedólgo dúmaja, <b>náglo</b> naprosílsja jejó provožátʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">and then one day I, not thinking any further, <b>impertinently</b> asked to accompany her</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наглухо.html>на́глухо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nágluxo</span>)

<ol><li>tightly, hermetically
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наглухо.html>на́глухо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заделать.html>заде́лать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nágluxo</b> zadélatʹ dverʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wall up a door</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:застегнуться.html>застегну́ться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наглухо.html>на́глухо</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zastegnutʹsja <b>nágluxo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">do up all one's buttons</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">наглъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naglŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*naglъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***наглядеться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наглядеться.html>нагляде́ться</a> (19992)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>гляде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gljadétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наглядеться.html>нагляде́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagljadétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to see enough
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>гляде́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наглядеться.html>нагляде́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gljadétʹ ne <b>nagljadétʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">never to get tired of looking (at someone/something)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жем</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наглядеться.html>нагляде́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My ne móžem <b>nagljadétʹsja</b> na étot vid.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We are not sick of this sight/view / We can't get enough of this view.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">We may not <b>see enough</b> of this sight/view.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to feast one's eyes</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>гляде́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gljadétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наглядность.html>нагля́дность</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nagljádnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>гля́д<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

***нагнетать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нагнетать.html>нагнета́ть</a> (25390)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">нагнет-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nagnet-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагнетать.html>нагнета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagnetátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нагнести́</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pump, to pressurize, to inflate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to aggravate, to exacerbate (negative emotions)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нагнета́ние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nagnetánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нагнета́тель</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nagnetátelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
